<h1 _ngcontent-lwc-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="CanvasRenderingContext2D对象"> CanvasRenderingContext2D对象 </h1>

<div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>从API version 4开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <p>使用CanvasRenderingContext2D在canvas画布组件上进行绘制，绘制对象可以是矩形、文本、图片等。</p> class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.2.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.2.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.2.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">描述</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#fillstyle">fillStyle</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">&lt;color&gt; | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasgradient">CanvasGradient</a> | CanvasPattern</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>指定绘制的填充色。</p>          <p>- 类型为&lt;color&gt;时，表示设置填充区域的颜色。</p>          <p>- 类型为CanvasGradient时，表示渐变对象，使用 createLinearGradient()方法创建。</p>          <p>- 类型为CanvasPattern时，使用 createPattern()方法创建。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#linewidth">lineWidth</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置绘制线条的宽度。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#strokestyle">strokeStyle</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">&lt;color&gt; | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasgradient">CanvasGradient</a> | CanvasPattern</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置描边的颜色。</p>          <p>- 类型为&lt;color&gt;时，表示设置描边使用的颜色。</p>          <p>- 类型为CanvasGradient时，表示渐变对象，使用 createLinearGradient()方法创建。</p>          <p>- 类型为CanvasPattern时，使用 createPattern()方法创建。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#linecap">lineCap</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>指定线端点的样式，可选值为：</p>          <p>- butt：线端点以方形结束。</p>          <p>- round：线端点以圆形结束。</p>          <p>- square：线端点以方形结束，该样式下会增加一个长度和线段厚度相同，宽度是线段厚度一半的矩形。</p>          <p>默认值：butt</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#linejoin">lineJoin</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>指定线段间相交的交点样式，可选值为：</p>          <p>- round：在线段相连处绘制一个扇形，扇形的圆角半径是线段的宽度。</p>          <p>- bevel：在线段相连处使用三角形为底填充， 每个部分矩形拐角独立。</p>          <p>- miter：在相连部分的外边缘处进行延伸，使其相交于一点，形成一个菱形区域，该属性可以通过设置miterLimit属性展现效果。</p>          <p>默认值：miter</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#miterlimit">miterLimit</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置斜接面限制值，该值指定了线条相交处内角和外角的距离。</p>          <p>默认值：10</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#font">font</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置文本绘制中的字体样式。</p>          <p>语法：ctx.font="font-style font-weight font-size font-family"<sup>5+</sup></p>          <p>- font-style(可选)，用于指定字体样式，支持如下几种样式：normal, italic。</p>          <p>- font-weight(可选)，用于指定字体的粗细，支持如下几种类型：normal, bold, bolder, lighter, 100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 600, 700, 800, 900。</p>          <p>- font-size(可选)，指定字号和行高，单位只支持px。</p>          <p>- font-family(可选)，指定字体系列，支持如下几种类型：sans-serif, serif, monospace。</p>          <p>默认值："normal normal 14px sans-serif"</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#textalign">textAlign</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置文本绘制中的文本对齐方式，可选值为：</p>          <p>- left：文本左对齐。</p>          <p>- right：文本右对齐。</p>          <p>- center：文本居中对齐。</p>          <p>- start：文本对齐界线开始的地方。</p>          <p>- end：文本对齐界线结束的地方。</p>          <p>ltr布局模式下start和left一致，rtl布局模式下start和right一致。</p>          <p>默认值：left</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#textbaseline">textBaseline</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置文本绘制中的水平对齐方式，可选值为：</p>          <p>- alphabetic：文本基线是标准的字母基线。</p>          <p>- top：文本基线在文本块的顶部。</p>          <p>- hanging：文本基线是悬挂基线。</p>          <p>- middle：文本基线在文本块的中间。</p>          <p>- ideographic：文字基线是表意字基线；如果字符本身超出了alphabetic 基线，那么ideographic基线位置在字符本身的底部。</p>          <p>- bottom：文本基线在文本块的底部。 与 ideographic 基线的区别在于 ideographic 基线不需要考虑下行字母。</p>          <p>默认值： alphabetic</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#globalalpha">globalAlpha</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置透明度，0.0为完全透明，1.0为完全不透明。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#linedashoffset">lineDashOffset</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置画布的虚线偏移量，精度为float。</p>          <p>默认值：0.0</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#globalcompositeoperation">globalCompositeOperation</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置合成操作的方式。类型字段可选值有source-over，source-atop，source-in，source-out，destination-over，destination-atop，destination-in，destination-out，lighter，copy，xor。具体请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#globalcompositeoperation">表 类型字段说明</a>。</p>          <p>默认值：source-over</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#shadowblur">shadowBlur</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>设置绘制阴影时的模糊级别，值越大越模糊，精度为float。</p>          <p>默认值：0.0</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#shadowcolor">shadowColor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">&lt;color&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置绘制阴影时的阴影颜色。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#shadowoffsetx">shadowOffsetX</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置绘制阴影时和原有对象的水平偏移值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#shadowoffsety">shadowOffsetY</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置绘制阴影时和原有对象的垂直偏移值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-canvasrenderingcontext2d#imagesmoothingenabled">imageSmoothingEnabled</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>用于设置绘制图片时是否进行图像平滑度调整，true为启用，false为不启用。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 689px;">     <h3 id="fillstyle" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">globalCompositeOperation<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="globalcompositeoperation" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>类型字段说明。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.3.1.3.1.1" width="50%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.3.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">source-over</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在现有绘制内容上显示新绘制内容，属于默认值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">source-atop</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在现有绘制内容顶部显示新绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">source-in</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在现有绘制内容中显示新绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">source-out</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在现有绘制内容之外显示新绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">destination-over</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在新绘制内容上方显示现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">destination-atop</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在新绘制内容顶部显示现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">destination-in</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在新绘制内容中显示现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">destination-out</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在新绘制内容外显示现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">lighter</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">显示新绘制内容和现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">copy</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">显示新绘制内容而忽略现有绘制内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">xor</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">使用异或操作对新绘制内容与现有绘制内容进行融合。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">方法<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="方法" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1267px;">     <h3 id="fillrect" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">fillRect<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fillrect" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fillRect(x: number, y: number, width:number, height: number): void</p>     <p>填充一个矩形。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">x</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定矩形左上角点的x坐标。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">y</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定矩形左上角点的y坐标。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">width</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定矩形的宽度。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">height</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定矩形的高度。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createPattern(image: Image, repetition: string): Object</p>     <p>通过指定图像和重复方式创建图片填充的模板。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" width="25%">设置图像重复的方式，取值为：'repeat'、'repeat-x'、 'repeat-y'、'no-repeat'。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> number, y: number): void</p>     <p>设置canvas画布的缩放变换属性，后续的绘制操作将按照缩放比例进行缩放。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">x</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置水平方向的缩放值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">y</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置垂直方向的缩放值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115757.29927455492272129186770198017213:50001231000000:2800:540643A5F16D863E452B88B0854098FB38585589E1796622F2CED68849244147.png" class="notEnlarge" width="67" height="64"></span></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1611px;">     <h3 id="transform" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">transform<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="transform" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>transform(scaleX: number, skewX: number, skewY: number, scale: number, translateX: number, translateY: number): void</p>     <p>transform方法对应一个变换矩阵，想对一个图形进行变化的时候，只要设置此变换矩阵相应的参数，对图形的各个定点的坐标分别乘以这个矩阵，就能得到新的定点的坐标。矩阵变换效果可叠加。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>变换后的坐标计算方式（x和y为变换前坐标，x'和y'为变换后坐标）：</p>       <ul>        <li>         <p>x' = scaleX * x + skewY * y + translateX</p></li>        <li>         <p>y' = skewX * x + scaleY * y + translateY</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">scaleX</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定水平缩放值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">skewX</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定水平倾斜值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">skewY</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定垂直倾斜值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">scaleY</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定垂直缩放值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">translateX</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定水平移动值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">translateY</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定垂直移动值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lwc-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setTransform<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">translate<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="translate" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>translate(x: number, y: number): void</p>     <p>移动当前坐标系的原点。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1284px;">     <h3 id="getimagedata" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getImageData<i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getImageData(sx: number, sy: number, sw: number, sh: number): ImageData</p>     <p>以当前canvas指定区域内的像素创建<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-components-canvas-imagedata">ImageData对象</a>。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sx</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要输出的区域的左上角x坐标。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sy</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要输出的区域的宽度。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sh</td>         <td
